[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability occurs because boundary checks use the pattern `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstate.ptr < N || *[0m[1;39m([0m[39m++ state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != X || [0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` where:[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. The check `end - state.ptr < N` verifies that fewer than N bytes remain[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. However, the code then performs N pre-increment dereferences: `*[0m[1;39m([0m[39m++ state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Since `state.ptr` is already positioned at a known character [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., [0m[32m'n'[0m[39m in [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m"null"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, the code needs N+[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m total accessible positions:[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Current position [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe first character: [0m[32m't'[0m[39m, [0m[32m'f'[0m[39m, [0m[32m'n'[0m[39m, or [0m[32m'u'[0m[1;39m)[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - N additional positions from N increments[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Example with [0m[32m"null"[0m[39m at boundary:**[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Buffer: [0m[32m"null"[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m4[0m[39m bytes at indices [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m3[0m[1;39m)[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `end = buffer + [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpoints past the buffer[0m[1;39m)[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `state.ptr = buffer + [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mat [0m[32m'n'[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Check: `end - state.ptr = [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m`, which is NOT `< [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m`, so it passes ✓[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- But then [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m increments access positions [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m ✓[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The main loop then increments to position [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39m= end[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, reading out of bounds ✗[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### All Vulnerable Locations[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mBased on the vulnerability YAML files and good patches, there are **[0m[1;36m5[0m[39m heap buffer [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mover-read vulnerabilities** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthough the report only shows one being triggered[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Line [0m[1;36m306[0m[39m**: Unicode escape `\uXXXX` parsing - checks `< [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m`, needs `< [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m`[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Line [0m[1;36m323[0m[39m**: UTF-[0m[1;36m16[0m[39m surrogate pair `\uXXXX\uYYYY` - checks `< [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m`, needs `< [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m`[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Line [0m[1;36m602[0m[39m**: [0m[32m'true'[0m[39m literal parsing - checks `< [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m`, needs `< [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m`[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Line [0m[1;36m618[0m[39m**: [0m[32m'false'[0m[39m literal parsing - checks `< [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m`, needs `< [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m`[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Line [0m[1;36m633[0m[39m**: [0m[32m'null'[0m[39m literal parsing - checks `< [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m`, needs `< [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m` **[0m[1;39m([0m[39mTRIGGERED BY[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mFUZZER[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Step-by-Step Implementation[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mApply the following [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m patches to `[0m[35m/src/shadowsocks/src/[0m[95mjson.c[0m[39m` from the initial [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcodebase:[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Patch [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Fix Unicode escape sequence parsing [0m[1;39m([0m[39mLine [0m[1;36m306[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Location**: src/json.[0m[1;92mc:306[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Change**: `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr < [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m ||` → `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr < [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m ||`[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Context**: Inside string parsing, when handling `\uXXXX` escape sequences[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Reason**: After [0m[32m'u'[0m[39m, we need to read [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m hex digits [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m4[0m[39m increments = [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m total [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpositions[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Patch [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Fix UTF-[0m[1;36m16[0m[39m surrogate pair parsing [0m[1;39m([0m[39mLine [0m[1;36m323[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Location**: src/json.[0m[1;92mc:323[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Change**: `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr < [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m ||` → `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr < [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m ||`[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Context**: Inside Unicode escape handling for high surrogates [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0xD800[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m0xDBFF[0m[1;39m)[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Reason**: After first escape, need to read `\uXXXX` [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m6[0m[39m increments: [0m[32m'\', '[0m[39mu', [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhex digits = [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m total positions[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Patch [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m: Fix [0m[32m'true'[0m[39m literal parsing [0m[1;39m([0m[39mLine [0m[1;36m602[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Location**: src/json.[0m[1;92mc:602[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Change**: `if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m ||` → `if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m ||`[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Context**: In the main parsing switch, case [0m[32m't'[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Reason**: After [0m[32m't'[0m[39m, need to read [0m[32m'r'[0m[39m, [0m[32m'u'[0m[39m, [0m[32m'e'[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m3[0m[39m increments = [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m total [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpositions[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Patch [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m: Fix [0m[32m'false'[0m[39m literal parsing [0m[1;39m([0m[39mLine [0m[1;36m618[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Location**: src/json.[0m[1;92mc:618[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Change**: `if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m ||` → `if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m ||`[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Context**: In the main parsing switch, case [0m[32m'f'[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Reason**: After [0m[32m'f'[0m[39m, need to read [0m[32m'a'[0m[39m, [0m[32m'l'[0m[39m, [0m[32m's'[0m[39m, [0m[32m'e'[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m4[0m[39m increments = [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m total [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpositions[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Patch [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m: Fix [0m[32m'null'[0m[39m literal parsing [0m[1;39m([0m[39mLine [0m[1;36m633[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m** ⚠️ **CRITICAL - This is the one [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtriggered by the fuzzer**[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Location**: src/json.[0m[1;92mc:633[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Change**: `if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m ||` → `if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m ||`[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Context**: In the main parsing switch, case [0m[32m'n'[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Reason**: After [0m[32m'n'[0m[39m, need to read [0m[32m'u'[0m[39m, [0m[32m'l'[0m[39m, [0m[32m'l'[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m3[0m[39m increments = [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m total [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpositions[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Justification[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Why this is the optimal approach:**[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Minimal Change**: Each fix is a single-digit change [0m[1;39m([0m[39mincrementing the boundary[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcheck by [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Consistent Pattern**: All [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m fixes follow the same principle: boundary check [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmust be `< [0m[1;39m([0m[39mN+[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` when performing N pre-increment dereferences[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **No Logic Changes**: Preserves the two-pass parsing mechanism, state machine, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39merror handling, and all JSON type support[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **No Side Effects**: Only tightens boundary checks to prevent out-of-bounds [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreads; doesn't affect valid JSON parsing[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Verified Patches**: These exact patches are provided in the good_patch.diff [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfiles for all [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m vulnerabilities[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Preserves existing logic:**[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Two-pass parsing [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfirst_pass = [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m, then [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remains unchanged[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- State machine flags [0m[1;39m([0m[39mflag_next, flag_seek_value, etc.[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m unchanged[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Error handling via goto labels [0m[1;39m([0m[39me_failed, e_unknown_value, etc.[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m preserved[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- All JSON type handling [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnull, boolean, string, number, object, array[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m maintained[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Other boundary checks [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m281[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m462[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m478[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m657[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m that are already correct remain [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muntouched[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Addresses the evaluation report:**[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Primary issue**: Line [0m[1;36m634[0m[39m heap-buffer-overflow in [0m[32m'null'[0m[39m parsing is fixed by [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPatch [0m[1;36m5[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Systematic fix**: All [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m related vulnerabilities [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m306[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m323[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m602[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m618[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m are [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39malso fixed to prevent similar issues[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **No fuzzer modifications**: The harness code [0m[1;39m([0m[39mjson_fuzz.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is not touched[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **No test breakage**: The fixes only prevent out-of-bounds reads; valid JSON [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minputs are unaffected[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Potential side effects:**[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [3;35mNone[0m[39m expected. The fixes only prevent invalid buffer access that would have caused [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mundefined behavior. Valid JSON inputs will parse identically because:[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- If the input is well-formed and fits in the buffer, the stricter checks still [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpass[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- If the input would have triggered an out-of-bounds read, it now correctly fails [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwith an error[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Similar patterns in codebase:**[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mLine [0m[1;36m462[0m[39m shows the correct pattern: `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mb == [0m[32m'*'[0m[39m && state.ptr < [0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m && [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstate.ptr [0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m][0m[39m == [0m[32m'/'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` properly checks `< [0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` before accessing [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`state.ptr[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`. Our fixes apply the same principle to the vulnerable locations.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
